          name: mysql

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to test/Deployment/mysqldeployment:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: mysqldeployment
  namespace: test
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: mysql
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAffinity:
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - labelSelector:
              matchExpressions:
              - key: app
                operator: In
                values:
                - wordpress
            topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
      containers:
      - env:
        - name: MYSQL_DATABASE
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_DATABASE
              name: mysqlenv
        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
              name: mysqlenv
        - name: MYSQL_USER
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_USER
              name: mysqlenv
        - name: MYSQL_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_PASSWORD
              name: mysqlenv
        image: mysql
        name: mysqlcon
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysqlvolume
      tolerations:
      - effect: NoSchedule
        key: tier
        operator: Equal
        value: production
      volumes:
      - name: mysqlvolume
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: mysqlpvc

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to mysql/Deployment/mysql-deployment:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app: mysql
  name: mysql-deployment
  namespace: mysql
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: mysql
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql
    spec:
      containers:
      - env:
        - name: MYSQL_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: user-password
              name: mysql-secrets
        - name: MYSQL_DATABASE
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: mysql-database
              name: mysql-configmap
        - name: MYSQL_USER
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: mysql-user
              name: mysql-configmap
        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: root-password
              name: mysql-secrets
        image: mysql:8.0
        livenessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - /bin/bash
            - -c
            - mysqladmin -p$MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD ping
          initialDelaySeconds: 20
          periodSeconds: 10
        name: mysql
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
        readinessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - /bin/bash
            - -c
            - mysql -p$MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD -h localhost -e 'SELECT 1'
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql/
          name: data-volume
      volumes:
      - name: data-volume
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: mysql-pvc

---

      volumes:

##### FILE: mysql-deployment74.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/mysql-gyeonggi:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: mysql-gyeonggi
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: mysql-gyeonggi
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql-gyeonggi
    spec:
      containers:
      - env:
        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
              name: mysql-secrets
        - name: MYSQL_DATABASE
          value: gyeonggi
        image: mysql:5.7
        livenessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - sh
            - -c
            - mysqladmin ping -u root -p$MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          initialDelaySeconds: 60
          periodSeconds: 10
        name: mysql-gyeonggi
        readinessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - sh
            - -c
            - mysqladmin ping -u root -p$MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          initialDelaySeconds: 60
          periodSeconds: 10
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-data
        - mountPath: /etc/mysql/conf.d
          name: config-volume
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - sh
        - -c
        - rm -rf /var/lib/mysql/*
        image: busybox
        name: init-mysql
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-data
      volumes:
      - name: mysql-data
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: mysql-gyeonggi-pvc
      - configMap:
          name: mysql-config
        name: config-volume

---

        name: mysql-gyeongsang

        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-data

  namespace: default

  strategy:

  template:

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/mysql:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  name: mysql
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: mysql
  serviceName: mysql
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql
    spec:
      containers:
      - env:
        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
              name: db-secret
        - name: MYSQL_USER
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_USER
              name: db-secret
        - name: MYSQL_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_PASSWORD
              name: db-secret
        - name: MYSQL_DATABASE
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_DATABASE
              name: db-config
        image: gulcantopcu/ckad-mysql:latest
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: mysql
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
        resources:
          limits:
            cpu: 500m
            memory: 512Mi
          requests:
            cpu: 5m
            memory: 500Mi
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-data
  volumeClaimTemplates:
  - metadata:
      name: mysql-data
    spec:
      accessModes:
      - ReadWriteOnce
      resources:
        requests:
          storage: 1Gi

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/mysql-stateful-set:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  name: mysql-stateful-set
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app-label: mysql-stateful-set
  serviceName: mysql
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app-label: mysql-stateful-set
    spec:
      containers:
      - envFrom:
        - secretRef:
            name: mysql-root-secrets
        image: mysql:latest
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: mysql-stateful-set
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
          name: mysql-data-volume
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-storage
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: mysql-init
        name: mysql-data-volume
  volumeClaimTemplates:
  - metadata:
      name: mysql-storage
    spec:
      accessModes:
      - ReadWriteOnce
      resources:
        requests:
          storage: 5G
      storageClassName: standard

##### FILE: mysql-statefulset14.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/mysql:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  labels:
    app: mysql
  name: mysql
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: mysql
  serviceName: mysql
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql
    spec:
      affinity:
        nodeAffinity:
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
            nodeSelectorTerms:
            - matchExpressions:
              - key: pool
                operator: In
                values:
                - db
      containers:
      - envFrom:
        - configMapRef:
            name: mysql-config
        - secretRef:
            name: mysql-secret
        image: mysql:8.0
        name: mysql
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
          name: mysql
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-persistent-storage
      tolerations:
      - effect: NoSchedule
        key: specialized
        operator: Equal
        value: stateful
  volumeClaimTemplates:
  - metadata:
      name: mysql-persistent-storage
    spec:
      accessModes:
      - ReadWriteOnce
      resources:
        requests:
          storage: 5Gi

---

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/StatefulSet/mysql-statefulset:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  name: mysql-statefulset
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: mysql
  serviceName: mysql-service
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql
    spec:
      containers:
      - env:
        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: mysql-root-password
              name: mysql-secret
        - name: MYSQL_USER
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: mysql-user
              name: mysql-secret
        - name: MYSQL_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: mysql-password
              name: mysql-secret
        image: mysql:8.0
        name: mysql
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
          name: mysql
        resources:
          limits:
            cpu: 512m
            memory: 512Mi
          requests:
            cpu: 512m
            memory: 512Mi
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-pv
        - mountPath: /etc/mysql/my.cnf
          name: config-volume
          subPath: my.cnf
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: mysql-config
        name: config-volume
  volumeClaimTemplates:
  - metadata:
      name: mysql-pv
    spec:
      accessModes:
      - ReadWriteOnce
      resources:
        requests:
          storage: 5Gi
      storageClassName: standard

##### FILE: mysql-store1_3.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/ConfigMap/mysql-store-initdb-config:
apiVersion: v1
data:
  initdb.sql: "CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS `store`;\n\nUSE `store`;\n\nCREATE TABLE
    IF NOT EXISTS cart (\n  id INTEGER NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,\n  usuario VARCHAR(60),\n
    \ isbn VARCHAR(60),\n  cantidad INTEGER,\n  PRIMARY KEY (id)\n);\n\n\n  DELIMITER
    //\n  CREATE PROCEDURE GetCartUser(usuario VARCHAR(60))\n  BEGIN\n    SELECT c.*
    FROM cart c WHERE c.usuario = usuario;\n  END //\n\n  CREATE PROCEDURE AddCartUser(usuario
    VARCHAR(60),isbn VARCHAR(60), unidades INTEGER)\n  BEGIN\n    DECLARE cant INTEGER
    DEFAULT NULL;\n    SELECT c.cantidad FROM cart c WHERE c.isbn = isbn AND c.usuario
    = usuario INTO cant;\n    if ISNULL(cant) then \n      INSERT INTO cart (usuario,isbn,cantidad)
    VALUES (usuario, isbn, 1);\n    ELSE\n      UPDATE cart c SET cantidad=unidades
    WHERE c.isbn = isbn AND c.usuario = usuario;\n    END if;\t\n  END //\n\n  CREATE
    PROCEDURE DeleteCartUser(usuario VARCHAR(60),isbn VARCHAR(60))\n  BEGIN\n    DELETE
    FROM cart c WHERE c.isbn = isbn AND c.usuario = usuario;\n  END //\n\n  CREATE
    PROCEDURE DeleteAllCartUser(usuario VARCHAR(60))\n  BEGIN\n    DELETE FROM cart
    c WHERE c.usuario = usuario;\n  END //\n\n  DELIMITER ;\n\n  INSERT INTO cart
    (usuario,isbn,cantidad) VALUES (\"student\", \"9789584276971\", 5);\n  INSERT
    INTO cart (usuario,isbn,cantidad) VALUES (\"juan\", \"9789584276971\", 1);\n  INSERT
    INTO cart (usuario,isbn,cantidad) VALUES (\"juan\", \"9789585190603\", 1);"
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: mysql-store-initdb-config
  namespace: default

---

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/mysql:

kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app: mysql
  name: mysql
  namespace: default

  replicas: 1

    matchLabels:
      app: mysql
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: mysql

      containers:
      - env:
        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:

              key: MYSQL_PASSWORD

        - name: MYSQL_DATABASE
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: MYSQL_DB
              name: mysql-config
        image: mysql:8
        name: mysql
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3306
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/lib/mysql
          name: mysql-persistent-storage
      volumes:
      - name: mysql-persistent-storage
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: mysql-pv-claim
